***настигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настигать.html>настига́ть</a> (14635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигнуть.html>насти́гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastígnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигать.html>настига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигнуть.html>насти́гнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">насти́чь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch up <i>(with)</i>, to come close <i>(to)</i>, to approach</li>
<li>to catch</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">FIXME</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догонять.html>догоня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dogonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сти́гнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stígnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигнуть.html>насти́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastígnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигать.html>настига́ть</a></b>)

***настолько.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настолько.html>насто́лько</a> (1346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настолько.html>насто́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>so, so much, as much, thus much</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настолько.html>насто́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>as</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настораживать.html>настора́живать</a> (15170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насторожить.html>насторожи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastorožítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настораживать.html>настора́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastoráživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насторожить.html>насторожи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to alert, to put on guard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настораживать.html>настора́живать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nastoráživatʹ úši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prick up one's ears</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настораживающий.html>настора́живающий</a> (15170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настораживающий.html>настора́живающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastoráživajuščij</span>)
</p>

***настороженность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настороженность.html>насторо́женность</a> (15815)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настороженность.html>насторо́женность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastoróžennostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настороженность.html>насторо́женности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настороженность.html>насторо́женности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настороженность.html>насторо́женностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vigilance, watchfulness, alertness</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожить.html>сторожи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">storožítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настоять.html>настоя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastojátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настаивать.html>наста́ивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to insist, to persist, to press on</li></ol>

<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastojáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>present
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nastojáščeje vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">present tense</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v nastojáščeje vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at present</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>догово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nastojáščij</b> dogovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this contract</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>true, real, genuine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nastojáščij</b> drug</i> ― <span class="e-translation">true friend</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">по-настоя́щему</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po-nastojáščemu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">properly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***настраивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настраивать.html>настра́ивать</a> (13625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настраивать.html>настра́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastráivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tune, to tune up, to adjust, to customize <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to modify</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:настраивать.html>настра́ивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рояль.html>роя́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nastráivatʹ</b> rojálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to tune up</b> a grand piano.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to incline <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prótiv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive against</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to incite, to make <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. someone sad/joyful</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
